   1
  const today = new Date();
  today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

  // Read the data file
  const didaData = await dv.io.load(".obsidian/plugins/Dida Sync/data.json");
  if (didaData) {
      const tasks = didaData.tasks;

      // --- Overdue Tasks ---
      const overdueTasks = tasks.filter(t => {
          if (t.status !== 0 || !t.dueDate) return false;
          const dueDate = new Date(t.dueDate);
          return dueDate < today;
      });

      if (overdueTasks.length > 0) {
          dv.header(2, "ğŸš¨ é€¾æœŸä»»åŠ¡");
          let displayTasks = [];
          for(let task of overdueTasks){
              let links = task.content.match(/(\[\[.+?\]\]|https?:\/\/\S+)/g) || [];
              let linkText = links.length > 0 ? "ğŸ”— " + links.join(" ") : "";
              displayTasks.push([ ] ${task.title} (æˆªæ­¢äº: ${new Date(task.dueDate).toLocaleDateString()}) ${linkText});
          }
          dv.list(displayTasks);
      }

      // --- Today's Completed Tasks ---
      const todayCompletedTasks = tasks.filter(t => {
          if (t.status !== 2 || !t.completedTime) return false;
          const completedDate = new Date(t.completedTime);
          completedDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
          return completedDate.getTime() === today.getTime();
      });

      if (todayCompletedTasks.length > 0) {
          dv.header(2, "âœ… ä»Šæ—¥å®Œæˆ");
          let displayTasks = [];
          for(let task of todayCompletedTasks){
              let links = task.content.match(/(\[\[.+?\]\]|https?:\/\/\S+)/g) || [];
              let linkText = links.length > 0 ? "ğŸ”— " + links.join(" ") : "";
              displayTasks.push([x] ${task.title} ${linkText});
          }
          dv.list(displayTasks);
      }

      if(overdueTasks.length === 0 && todayCompletedTasks.length === 0){
          dv.paragraph("æ— ç›¸å…³ä»»åŠ¡ã€‚");
      }
  } else {
      dv.paragraph("æ— æ³•åŠ è½½æ»´ç­”æ¸…å•æ•°æ®ã€‚");
  }

      // --- Overdue Tasks ---
      const overdueTasks = tasks.filter(t => {
          if (t.status !== 0 || !t.dueDate) return false;
          const dueDate = new Date(t.dueDate);
          return dueDate < today;
      });

      if (overdueTasks.length > 0) {
          dv.header(2, "ğŸš¨ é€¾æœŸä»»åŠ¡");

      const todayCompletedTasks = tasks.filter(t => {
          if (t.status !== 2 || !t.completedTime) return false;
          const completedDate = new Date(t.completedTime);
          completedDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
          return completedDate.getTime() === today.getTime();
      });

          dv.header(2, "âœ… ä»Šæ—¥å®Œæˆ");

              displayTasks.push([x] ${task.title} ${linkText});
          }
          dv.list(displayTasks);
      }

          dv.paragraph("æ— ç›¸å…³ä»»åŠ¡ã€‚");

   1
  const today = new Date();
  today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

  // Read the data file
  const didaData = await dv.io.load(".obsidian/plugins/Dida Sync/data.json");
  if (didaData && didaData.tasks) {
      const tasks = didaData.tasks;

      // --- Overdue Tasks ---
      const overdueTasks = tasks.filter(t => {
          if (t.status !== 0 || !t.dueDate) return false;
          const dueDate = new Date(t.dueDate);
          return dueDate < today;
      });

      if (overdueTasks.length > 0) {
          dv.header(3, "ğŸš¨ é€¾æœŸä»»åŠ¡");
          let displayTasks = [];
          for(let task of overdueTasks){
              let links = task.content.match(/(\[\[.+?\]\]|https?:\/\/\S+)/g) || [];
              let linkText = links.length > 0 ? "ğŸ”— " + links.join(" ") : "";
              displayTasks.push([ ] ${task.title} (æˆªæ­¢äº: ${new Date(task.dueDate).toLocaleDateString()}) ${linkText});
          }
          dv.list(displayTasks);
      }

      // --- Today's Completed Tasks ---
      const todayCompletedTasks = tasks.filter(t => {
          if (t.status !== 2 || !t.completedTime) return false;
          const todayDateString = today.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
          return t.completedTime.startsWith(todayDateString);
      });

      if (todayCompletedTasks.length > 0) {
          dv.header(3, "âœ… ä»Šæ—¥å®Œæˆ");
          let displayTasks = [];
          for(let task of todayCompletedTasks){
              let links = task.content.match(/(\[\[.+?\]\]|https?:\/\/\S+)/g) || [];
              let linkText = links.length > 0 ? "ğŸ”— " + links.join(" ") : "";
              displayTasks.push([x] ${task.title} ${linkText});
          }
          dv.list(displayTasks);
      }

      if(overdueTasks.length === 0 && todayCompletedTasks.length === 0){
          dv.paragraph("ğŸ‘ æ— é€¾æœŸä»»åŠ¡ï¼Œä»Šæ—¥æ— å·²å®Œæˆä»»åŠ¡ã€‚");
      }
  } else {
      dv.paragraph("âŒ æ— æ³•åŠ è½½æ»´ç­”æ¸…å•æ•°æ®ã€‚è¯·æ£€æŸ¥ .obsidian/plugins/Dida Sync/data.json æ–‡ä»¶æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨ã€‚");
  }
